4.5 Охранник v2 (оптимизированный)
python
# src/agents/guardian.py
"""
ОХРАННИК v2 - Оптимизированный с внешним Vault (опционально)
"""

import asyncio
import logging
from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuple
from datetime import datetime
import json
import hashlib
import secrets
import os

from src.api.llm_router import llm_router
from src.tools.database_tools import DatabaseTools
from src.core.config import config

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class SecretVault:
    """Хранилище секретов с AES-256-GCM шифрованием"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        master_key = os.getenv("VAULT_MASTER_KEY")
        if not master_key:
            raise ValueError("VAULT_MASTER_KEY not set in environment")
        
        try:
            from cryptography.fernet import Fernet
            # Для Fernet нужен ключ в base64 формате длиной 32 байта
            self.cipher = Fernet(master_key.encode())
            logger.info("Secret Vault initialized with Fernet encryption")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Failed to initialize Fernet cipher: {e}")
            raise
    
    async def store_secret(
        self, 
        key: str, 
        value: str, 
        db_tools, 
        owner_id: int, 
        allowed_agent_ids: List[int]
    ) -> Dict:
        """Сохранение секрета"""
        
        try:
            encrypted = self.cipher.encrypt(value.encode())
            
            await db_tools.execute("db_execute", {
                "query": """
                    INSERT INTO secrets_vault
                    (secret_name, secret_type, encrypted_value, owner_id, allowed_agent_ids)
                    VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5)
                    ON CONFLICT (secret_name) DO UPDATE
                    SET encrypted_value = EXCLUDED.encrypted_value,
                        last_accessed = NOW(),
                        allowed_agent_ids = EXCLUDED.allowed_agent_ids
                """,
                "params": [key, "generic", encrypted, owner_id, allowed_agent_ids]
            })
            
            logger.info(f"Secret stored: {key}")
            
            return {"success": True, "key": key}
        
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error storing secret: {e}", exc_info=True)
            return {"success": False, "error": str(e)}
    
    async def retrieve_secret(
        self, 
        key: str, 
        requesting_agent_id: int, 
        db_tools
    ) -> Optional[str]:
        """Получение секрета с проверкой прав"""
        
        try:
            result = await db_tools.execute("db_query", {
                "query": """
                    SELECT encrypted_value, allowed_agent_ids, owner_id
                    FROM secrets_vault
                    WHERE secret_name = $1
                """,
                "params": [key]
            })
            
            if not result.get('success') or not result.get('data'):
                logger.warning(f"Secret not found: {key}")
                return None
            
            row = result['data'][0]
            encrypted = row['encrypted_value']
            allowed_ids = row['allowed_agent_ids'] or []
            owner_id = row['owner_id']
            
            # Проверка прав (owner всегда имеет доступ)
            if requesting_agent_id not in allowed_ids and requesting_agent_id != owner_id:
                logger.warning(f"Access denied to secret {key} for agent_id {requesting_agent_id}")
                return None
            
            # Дешифрование
            decrypted = self.cipher.decrypt(encrypted)
            
            # Обновление метрик
            await db_tools.execute("db_execute", {
                "query": """
                    UPDATE secrets_vault
                    SET last_accessed = NOW(), access_count = access_count + 1
                    WHERE secret_name = $1
                """,
                "params": [key]
            })
            
            return decrypted.decode('utf-8')
        
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error retrieving secret: {e}", exc_info=True)
            return None

class SecurityMonitor:
    """Мониторинг безопасности"""
    
    def __init__(self, db_tools):
        self.db_tools = db_tools
        self.failed_attempts = {}
        self.blocked_ips = set()
        
        # Загрузка конфигурации
        security_cfg = config.get("guardian.security", {})
        self.detection_rules = {
            "brute_force": {
                "threshold": security_cfg.get('brute_force_threshold', 5),
                "window_seconds": security_cfg.get('brute_force_window_seconds', 60)
            },
            "anomalous_behavior": {
                "threshold": security_cfg.get('anomaly_threshold', 100),
                "window_seconds": security_cfg.get('anomaly_window_seconds', 300)
            }
        }
    
    async def check_request(
        self, 
        ip: str, 
        agent_id: int, 
        endpoint: str
    ) -> Tuple[bool, Optional[str]]:
        """Проверка входящего запроса"""
        
        # Проверка блокировки IP
        if ip in self.blocked_ips:
            logger.warning(f"Blocked IP attempted access: {ip}")
            await self._log_security_event("blocked_ip_attempt", ip, endpoint)
            return False, "IP blocked"
        
        # Обнаружение аномалий
        is_anomalous = await self._detect_anomalous_behavior(ip, endpoint)
        
        if is_anomalous:
            await self._handle_anomaly(ip, endpoint)
            return False, "Anomalous behavior detected"
        
        return True, None
    
    async def record_failed_attempt(self, ip: str, reason: str):
        """Регистрация неудачной попытки"""
        
        now = datetime.now()
        
        if ip not in self.failed_attempts:
            self.failed_attempts[ip] = []
        
        self.failed_attempts[ip].append({"timestamp": now, "reason": reason})
        
        # Очистка старых записей
        self.failed_attempts[ip] = [
            a for a in self.failed_attempts[ip]
            if (now - a['timestamp']).total_seconds() < 3600
        ]
        
        # Проверка на brute-force
        recent_count = len([
            a for a in self.failed_attempts[ip]
            if (now - a['timestamp']).total_seconds() < self.detection_rules['brute_force']['window_seconds']
        ])
        
        if recent_count >= self.detection_rules['brute_force']['threshold']:
            await self._block_ip(ip, "brute_force")
    
    async def _block_ip(self, ip: str, reason: str):
        """Блокировка IP"""
        
        self.blocked_ips.add(ip)
        logger.critical(f"IP blocked: {ip} (reason: {reason})")
        
        try:
            await self._log_security_event("ip_blocked", ip, reason)
            
            # Сохранение в БД
            await self.db_tools.execute("db_execute", {
                "query": """
                    INSERT INTO blocked_entities (entity_type, entity_id, blocked_by, reason, block_type)
                    VALUES ('ip', $1, (SELECT id FROM agents WHERE name = 'Guardian'), $2, 'temporary')
                """,
                "params": [ip, reason]
            })
            
            await self._send_security_alert({
                "type": "ip_blocked",
                "ip": ip,
                "reason": reason,
                "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat()
            })
        
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error blocking IP: {e}", exc_info=True)
    
    async def _detect_anomalous_behavior(self, ip: str, endpoint: str) -> bool:
        """Обнаружение аномалий"""
        
        try:
            result = await self.db_tools.execute("db_query", {
                "query": """
                    SELECT COUNT(*) as request_count
                    FROM audit_log
                    WHERE ip_address = $1::inet
                      AND timestamp > NOW() - INTERVAL '5 minutes'
                """,
                "params": [ip]
            })
            
            if result.get('success') and result.get('data'):
                count = result['data'][0]['request_count']
                threshold = self.detection_rules['anomalous_behavior']['threshold']
                if count > threshold:
                    return True
        
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error detecting anomalies: {e}")
        
        return False
    
    async def _handle_anomaly(self, ip: str, endpoint: str):
        """Обработка аномалии"""
        logger.warning(f"Anomalous behavior from {ip} on {endpoint}")
        await self._log_security_event("anomaly_detected", ip, endpoint)
    
    async def _log_security_event(self, event_type: str, ip: str, details: str):
        """Логирование события безопасности"""
        
        try:
            await self.db_tools.execute("db_execute", {
                "query": """
                    INSERT INTO security_events (event_type, ip_address, details)
                    VALUES ($1, $2::inet, $3)
                """,
                "params": [event_type, ip, details]
            })
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error logging security event: {e}")
    
    async def _send_security_alert(self, alert: Dict):
        """Отправка алерта через N8N webhook"""
        
        webhook_url = config.get("n8n.webhooks.security_alerts")
        
        if not webhook_url:
            logger.warning("Security webhook URL not configured")
            return
        
        try:
            import aiohttp
            
            async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:
                await session.post(
                    webhook_url, 
                    json=alert,
                    timeout=aiohttp.ClientTimeout(total=5)
                )
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Failed to send security alert: {e}")

class IncidentAnalyzer:
    """Анализатор инцидентов - Root Cause Analysis"""
    
    def __init__(self, db_tools):
        self.db_tools = db_tools
    
    async def analyze_incident(self, incident: Dict) -> Dict:
        """
        Полный анализ инцидента
        
        Pipeline:
        1. Сбор контекста
        2. Root Cause Analysis
        3. Определение мер предотвращения
        4. Сохранение в журнал
        """
        
        incident_type = incident.get('type')
        service = incident.get('service')
        
        logger.info(f"Analyzing incident: {incident_type} on {service}")
        
        try:
            # 1. Сбор контекста
            context = await self._gather_incident_context(incident)
            
            # 2. RCA через Groq
            rca = await self._perform_rca(incident, context)
            
            # 3. Меры предотвращения
            prevention = await self._determine_prevention_measures(rca)
            
            # 4. Сохранение в журнал
            incident_id = await self._save_to_incident_journal(incident, rca, prevention)
            
            return {
                "incident_id": incident_id,
                "root_cause": rca,
                "prevention": prevention
            }
        
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error analyzing incident: {e}", exc_info=True)
            return {
                "incident_id": -1,
                "root_cause": {"error": str(e)},
                "prevention": []
            }
    
    async def _gather_incident_context(self, incident: Dict) -> Dict:
        """Сбор контекста инцидента"""
        
        service = incident.get('service')
        
        try:
            # Получение логов из audit_log
            logs_result = await self.db_tools.execute("db_query", {
                "query": """
                    SELECT action_type, resource, granted, reason, timestamp
                    FROM audit_log
                    WHERE timestamp > NOW() - INTERVAL '1 hour'
                    ORDER BY timestamp DESC
                    LIMIT 50
                """
            })
            
            return {
                "logs": logs_result.get('data', []),
                "metrics": incident.get('metrics', {}),
                "system_state": incident.get('system_state', {})
            }
        
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error gathering context: {e}")
            return {"logs": [], "metrics": {}, "system_state": {}}
    
    async def _perform_rca(self, incident: Dict, context: Dict) -> Dict:
        """Root Cause Analysis через Groq"""
        
        prompt = f"""
Проведи Root Cause Analysis (RCA) инцидента.

Инцидент: {json.dumps(incident, ensure_ascii=False)}
Контекст: {json.dumps(context, ensure_ascii=False)[:2000]}

JSON:
{{
  "root_cause": "...",
  "category": "external | code_error | overload | config | security",
  "probability_of_recurrence": 0.X,
  "analysis": "..."
}}
"""
        
        try:
            response = await llm_router.generate("Guardian", prompt, temperature=0.1)
            
            if response['success']:
                return json.loads(response['text'])
        
        except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
            logger.error(f"Failed to parse RCA JSON: {e}")
            return {"root_cause": response.get('text', 'Unknown'), "category": "unknown"}
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error in RCA: {e}", exc_info=True)
            return {"root_cause": str(e), "category": "error"}
        
        return {}
    
    async def _determine_prevention_measures(self, rca: Dict) -> List[str]:
        """Определение мер предотвращения"""
        
        prompt = f"""
На основе RCA определи меры предотвращения:
{json.dumps(rca, ensure_ascii=False)}

Список конкретных мер (JSON array): ["мера 1", "мера 2", ...]
"""
        
        try:
            response = await llm_router.generate("Guardian", prompt)
            
            if response['success']:
                return json.loads(response['text'])
        
        except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
            logger.error(f"Failed to parse prevention measures: {e}")
            return [response.get('text', '')]
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error determining prevention: {e}")
            return []
        
        return []
    
    async def _save_to_incident_journal(
        self, 
        incident: Dict, 
        rca: Dict, 
        prevention: List[str]
    ) -> int:
        """Сохранение в журнал инцидентов"""
        
        try:
            result = await self.db_tools.execute("db_execute", {
                "query": """
                    INSERT INTO incident_journal 
                    (incident_type, service, incident_data, rca, prevention_measures)
                    VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5)
                    RETURNING id
                """,
                "params": [
                    incident.get('type'),
                    incident.get('service'),
                    json.dumps(incident),
                    json.dumps(rca),
                    json.dumps(prevention)
                ]
            })
            
            if result.get('success') and result.get('data'):
                return result['data'][0]['id']
        
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error saving incident journal: {e}", exc_info=True)
        
        return -1

class GuardianAgent:
    """
    Guardian - безопасность, аудит, защита
    
    КРИТИЧЕСКИЕ ПРАВИЛА:
    - НЕ может блокировать Формулятора
    - Абсолютное подчинение Формулятору
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.name = "Guardian"
        self.tier = 1
        
        self.db_tools = DatabaseTools()
        self.secret_vault = SecretVault()
        self.security_monitor = SecurityMonitor(self.db_tools)
        self.incident_analyzer = IncidentAnalyzer(self.db_tools)
        
        self.formulator_name = "Formulator"
        
        logger.info("Guardian initialized")
    
    async def initialize(self):
        """Инициализация"""
        # Загрузка правил безопасности из БД
        try:
            result = await self.db_tools.execute("db_query", {
                "query": """
                    SELECT policy_name, rules, enabled
                    FROM security_policies
                    WHERE enabled = true
                """
            })
            
            if result.get('success'):
                logger.info(f"Loaded {len(result.get('data', []))} security policies")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error loading security policies: {e}")
    
    async def execute_action(self, action: str, params: Dict) -> Dict:
        """Выполнение действия от Формулятора"""
        
        try:
            if action == "validate_security":
                return await self.validate_security(params)
            elif action == "log_incident":
                return await self.log_and_analyze_incident(params)
            elif action == "authorize":
                return await self.authorize_action(params)
            elif action == "block_agent":
                return await self.block_agent(params)
            elif action == "unblock_agent":
                return await self.unblock_agent(params)
            elif action == "store_secret":
                return await self.store_secret(params)
            elif action == "retrieve_secret":
                return await self.retrieve_secret(params)
            
            return {"success": False, "error": f"Unknown action: {action}"}
        
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error in execute_action: {e}", exc_info=True)
            return {"success": False, "error": str(e)}
    
    async def validate_security(self, params: Dict) -> Dict:
        """Проверка безопасности агента"""
        
        agent_name = params.get('agent_name')
        
        logger.info(f"Validating security for: {agent_name}")
        
        try:
            checks = await self._run_security_checks(agent_name)
            all_passed = all(check['passed'] for check in checks)
            
            return {
                "success": True, 
                "agent_name": agent_name, 
                "validated": all_passed, 
                "checks": checks
            }
        
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error validating security: {e}", exc_info=True)
            return {"success": False, "error": str(e)}
    
    async def log_and_analyze_incident(self, params: Dict) -> Dict:
        """Логирование и анализ инцидента"""
        
        incident = params.get('incident', {})
        
        logger.info(f"Logging incident: {incident.get('type')}")
        
        try:
            # Полный анализ
            analysis = await self.incident_analyzer.analyze_incident(incident)
            
            # Логирование в emergency_logs
            await self.db_tools.execute("db_execute", {
                "query": """
                    INSERT INTO emergency_logs (severity, message, source, details)
                    VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4)
                """,
                "params": [
                    incident.get('severity', 5),
                    incident.get('type'),
                    incident.get('service'),
                    json.dumps(analysis)
                ]
            })
            
            return {
                "success": True, 
                "incident_id": analysis['incident_id'], 
                "analysis": analysis
            }
        
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error logging incident: {e}", exc_info=True)
            return {"success": False, "error": str(e)}
    
    async def authorize_action(self, params: Dict) -> Dict:
        """Авторизация действия агента"""
        
        agent_name = params.get('agent_name')
        action_type = params.get('action_type')
        resource = params.get('resource')
        
        # Формулятор всегда авторизован
        if agent_name == self.formulator_name:
            await self._audit_action(agent_name, action_type, resource, True, "Formulator privilege")
            return {"authorized": True, "reason": "Formulator privilege"}
        
        try:
            # Получить agent_id
            agent_id_result = await self.db_tools.execute("db_query", {
                "query": "SELECT id FROM agents WHERE name = $1",
                "params": [agent_name]
            })
            
            if not agent_id_result.get('success') or not agent_id_result.get('data'):
                return {"authorized": False, "reason": "Agent not found"}
            
            agent_id = agent_id_result['data'][0]['id']
            
            # Проверка блокировок
            is_blocked = await self._check_if_blocked(agent_id)
            
            if is_blocked:
                await self._audit_action(agent_name, action_type, resource, False, "Agent blocked")
                return {"authorized": False, "reason": "Agent blocked"}
            
            # Применение политик
            policy_result = await self._apply_security_policies(agent_name, action_type, resource)
            
            if not policy_result['allowed']:
                await self._audit_action(agent_name, action_type, resource, False, policy_result['reason'])
                return {"authorized": False, "reason": policy_result['reason']}
            
            # Оценка рисков
            risk_score = await self._calculate_risk(agent_name, action_type, resource)
            
            high_risk_threshold = config.get("guardian.security.high_risk_threshold", 0.8)
            
            if risk_score > high_risk_threshold:
                await self._notify_formulator({
                    "type": "high_risk_action",
                    "agent": agent_name,
                    "action": action_type,
                    "resource": resource,
                    "risk_score": risk_score
                })
                
                await self._audit_action(agent_name, action_type, resource, False, f"High risk ({risk_score})", risk_score)
                
                return {
                    "authorized": False, 
                    "reason": "High risk - requires Formulator approval", 
                    "status": "pending_approval"
                }
            
            # Разрешено
            await self._audit_action(agent_name, action_type, resource, True, "Policy compliant", risk_score)
            
            return {"authorized": True, "risk_score": risk_score}
        
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error in authorization: {e}", exc_info=True)
            return {"authorized": False, "reason": f"Authorization error: {str(e)}"}
    
    async def block_agent(self, params: Dict) -> Dict:
        """
        Блокировка агента
        КРИТИЧНО: НЕ может заблокировать Формулятора!
        """
        
        agent_name = params.get('agent_name')
        reason = params.get('reason')
        requester = params.get('requester', 'Guardian')
        
        # КРИТИЧЕСКАЯ ПРОВЕРКА
        if agent_name == self.formulator_name or agent_name.lower() == "formulator":
            logger.critical(f"ATTEMPTED TO BLOCK FORMULATOR BY {requester} - REJECTED!")
            return {
                "success": False,
                "error": "Cannot block Formulator",
                "rule": "Guardian cannot block Formulator - Absolute rule"
            }
        
        logger.warning(f"Blocking agent: {agent_name} (reason: {reason})")
        
        try:
            # Блокировка
            await self.db_tools.execute("db_execute", {
                "query": """
                    UPDATE agents 
                    SET active = false, updated_at = NOW() 
                    WHERE name = $1
                """,
                "params": [agent_name]
            })
            
            # Логирование
            await self.db_tools.execute("db_execute", {
                "query": """
                    INSERT INTO agent_blocks (agent_id, reason, blocked_by)
                    VALUES (
                        (SELECT id FROM agents WHERE name = $1),
                        $2, 
                        (SELECT id FROM agents WHERE name = 'Guardian')
                    )
                """,
                "params": [agent_name, reason]
            })
            
            # Уведомление Формулятора
            await self._notify_formulator({
                "type": "agent_blocked",
                "agent_name": agent_name,
                "reason": reason,
                "awaiting_decision": True
            })
            
            return {"success": True, "agent_name": agent_name, "blocked": True}
        
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error blocking agent: {e}", exc_info=True)
            return {"success": False, "error": str(e)}
    
    async def unblock_agent(self, params: Dict) -> Dict:
        """Разблокировка агента (ТОЛЬКО по приказу Формулятора)"""
        
        agent_name = params.get('agent_name')
        requester = params.get('requester')
        
        # ПРОВЕРКА: только Формулятор может разблокировать
        if requester != self.formulator_name:
            logger.warning(f"Unauthorized unblock attempt by {requester} for {agent_name}")
            return {"success": False, "error": "Only Formulator can unblock agents"}
        
        logger.info(f"Unblocking agent: {agent_name} (by Formulator)")
        
        try:
            await self.db_tools.execute("db_execute", {
                "query": """
                    UPDATE agents 
                    SET active = true, updated_at = NOW() 
                    WHERE name = $1
                """,
                "params": [agent_name]
            })
            
            await self.db_tools.execute("db_execute", {
                "query": """
                    UPDATE agent_blocks 
                    SET unblocked_at = NOW(), 
                        unblocked_by = (SELECT id FROM agents WHERE name = 'Formulator')
                    WHERE agent_id = (SELECT id FROM agents WHERE name = $1) 
                      AND unblocked_at IS NULL
                """,
                "params": [agent_name]
            })
            
            return {"success": True, "agent_name": agent_name, "unblocked": True}
        
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error unblocking agent: {e}", exc_info=True)
            return {"success": False, "error": str(e)}
    
    async def store_secret(self, params: Dict) -> Dict:
        """Сохранение секрета"""
        
        key = params.get('key')
        value = params.get('value')
        owner_name = params.get('owner', 'system')
        allowed_agent_names = params.get('allowed_agents', [])
        
        try:
            # Получить owner_id
            owner_result = await self.db_tools.execute("db_query", {
                "query": "SELECT id FROM agents WHERE name = $1",
                "params": [owner_name]
            })
            
            owner_id = owner_result['data'][0]['id'] if owner_result.get('success') and owner_result.get('data') else 1
            
            # Получить allowed_agent_ids
            allowed_ids = []
            if allowed_agent_names:
                allowed_result = await self.db_tools.execute("db_query", {
                    "query": "SELECT id FROM agents WHERE name = ANY($1)",
                    "params": [allowed_agent_names]
                })
                
                if allowed_result.get('success'):
                    allowed_ids = [row['id'] for row in allowed_result.get('data', [])]
            
            result = await self.secret_vault.store_secret(key, value, self.db_tools, owner_id, allowed_ids)
            
            return result
        
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error storing secret: {e}", exc_info=True)
            return {"success": False, "error": str(e)}
    
    async def retrieve_secret(self, params: Dict) -> Dict:
        """Получение секрета"""
        
        key = params.get('key')
        requesting_agent_name = params.get('requesting_agent')
        
        try:
            # Получить agent_id
            agent_result = await self.db_tools.execute("db_query", {
                "query": "SELECT id FROM agents WHERE name = $1",
                "params": [requesting_agent_name]
            })
            
            if not agent_result.get('success') or not agent_result.get('data'):
                return {"success": False, "error": "Agent not found"}
            
            agent_id = agent_result['data'][0]['id']
            
            value = await self.secret_vault.retrieve_secret(key, agent_id, self.db_tools)
            
            if value:
                return {"success": True, "secret_value": value}
            
            return {"success": False, "error": "Access denied or secret not found"}
        
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error retrieving secret: {e}", exc_info=True)
            return {"success": False, "error": str(e)}
    
    # Вспомогательные методы
    
    async def _run_security_checks(self, agent_name: str) -> List[Dict]:
        """Проверки безопасности"""
        
        checks = []
        
        try:
            # Проверка tier
            tier_check = await self._check_tier_compliance(agent_name)
            checks.append(tier_check)
            
            # Проверка allowed_tools
            tools_check = await self._check_tools_safety(agent_name)
            checks.append(tools_check)
            
            # Проверка активности
            activity_check = await self._check_suspicious_activity(agent_name)
            checks.append(activity_check)
        
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error running security checks: {e}")
            checks.append({"check": "error", "passed": False, "details": str(e)})
        
        return checks
    
    async def _check_tier_compliance(self, agent_name: str) -> Dict:
        """Проверка соответствия tier"""
        
        try:
            result = await self.db_tools.execute("db_query", {
                "query": "SELECT tier, allowed_tools FROM agents WHERE name = $1",
                "params": [agent_name]
            })
            
            if result.get('success') and result.get('data'):
                agent = result['data'][0]
                
                if agent['tier'] == 2:
                    restricted = ["docker_container_manage", "db_execute", "agent_delete"]
                    has_restricted = any(tool in (agent['allowed_tools'] or []) for tool in restricted)
                    
                    return {
                        "check": "tier_compliance",
                        "passed": not has_restricted,
                        "details": "Tier 2 has restricted tools" if has_restricted else "OK"
                    }
        
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error in tier compliance check: {e}")
        
        return {"check": "tier_compliance", "passed": True}
    
    async def _check_tools_safety(self, agent_name: str) -> Dict:
        """Проверка безопасности инструментов"""
        # TODO: Implement actual tool safety checks
        return {"check": "tools_safety", "passed": True}
    
    async def _check_suspicious_activity(self, agent_name: str) -> Dict:
        """Проверка подозрительной активности"""
        
        try:
            result = await self.db_tools.execute("db_query", {
                "query": """
                    SELECT COUNT(*) as failed_count
                    FROM agent_logs
                    WHERE agent_id = (SELECT id FROM agents WHERE name = $1)
                      AND success = false
                      AND executed_at > NOW() - INTERVAL '1 hour'
                """,
                "params": [agent_name]
            })
            
            if result.get('success') and result.get('data'):
                failed_count = result['data'][0]['failed_count']
                suspicious = failed_count > 20
                
                return {
                    "check": "suspicious_activity",
                    "passed": not suspicious,
                    "details": f"{failed_count} failures in last hour"
                }
        
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error checking suspicious activity: {e}")
        
        return {"check": "suspicious_activity", "passed": True}
    
    async def _check_if_blocked(self, agent_id: int) -> bool:
        """Проверка блокировки"""
        
        try:
            result = await self.db_tools.execute("db_query", {
                "query": """
                    SELECT id FROM blocked_entities
                    WHERE entity_type = 'agent' 
                      AND entity_id = $1::text
                      AND unblocked_at IS NULL
                """,
                "params": [str(agent_id)]
            })
            
            return len(result.get('data', [])) > 0
        
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error checking block status: {e}")
            return False
    
    async def _apply_security_policies(
        self, 
        agent_name: str, 
        action_type: str, 
        resource: str
    ) -> Dict:
        """Применение политик безопасности"""
        
        # TODO: Implement comprehensive policy engine
        # For now, simple allow-all except for critical resources
        
        if 'secret' in resource.lower() and action_type == 'delete':
            return {"allowed": False, "reason": "Secret deletion not allowed"}
        
        return {"allowed": True, "reason": "Policy compliant"}
    
    async def _calculate_risk(
        self, 
        agent: str, 
        action: str, 
        resource: str
    ) -> float:
        """Оценка риска"""
        
        risk = 0.0
        
        # Риск по типу действия
        action_risk = {
            'read': 0.1, 'write': 0.3, 'delete': 0.7,
            'execute': 0.5, 'deploy': 0.6, 'modify_policy': 0.9
        }
        risk += action_risk.get(action, 0.5)
        
        # Риск по типу ресурса
        if 'secret' in resource.lower():
            risk += 0.3
        if 'agent' in resource.lower():
            risk += 0.2
        
        return min(risk, 1.0)
    
    async def _audit_action(
        self, 
        agent: str, 
        action: str, 
        resource: str, 
        granted: bool, 
        reason: str, 
        risk_score: float = 0.0
    ):
        """Аудит действия"""
        
        try:
            await self.db_tools.execute("db_execute", {
                "query": """
                    INSERT INTO audit_log
                    (agent_id, action_type, resource, granted, reason, risk_score)
                    VALUES (
                        (SELECT id FROM agents WHERE name = $1),
                        $2, $3, $4, $5, $6
                    )
                """,
                "params": [agent, action, resource, granted, reason, risk_score]
            })
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error auditing action: {e}")
    
    async def _notify_formulator(self, notification: Dict):
        """Уведомление Формулятора"""
        
        try:
            await self.db_tools.execute("db_execute", {
                "query": """
                    INSERT INTO formulator_notifications (notification_type, content, priority)
                    VALUES ($1, $2, $3)
                """,
                "params": [
                    notification.get('type'), 
                    json.dumps(notification),
                    'high' if notification.get('type') == 'agent_blocked' else 'medium'
                ]
            })
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error notifying Formulator: {e}")
